#### <a name="722-tablechecksum-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-1379">Campo 7.2.2 TableChecksum</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1379">7.2.2 TableChecksum Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1380">Il campo TableChecksum contiene il checksum della tabella del case che descrive i campi FirstCluster e DATALENGTH.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1380">The TableChecksum field contains the checksum of the Up-case Table (which the FirstCluster and DataLength fields describe).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1381">Le implementazioni devono verificare che il contenuto di questo campo sia valido prima di utilizzare la tabella del case.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1381">Implementations shall verify the contents of this field are valid prior to using the Up-case Table.</span></span>

<div id="figure-3-tablechecksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1382">**Figura 3 calcolo di TableChecksum**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1382">**Figure 3 TableChecksum Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt32 TableChecksum
(
    UCHAR  * Table,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-case table
    UInt64   DataLength
)
{
    UInt32 Checksum = 0;
    UInt64 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < DataLength; Index++)
    {
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x80000000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) + (UInt32)Table[Index];
    }

    return Checksum;
}
```

#### <a name="723-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-1383">Campo 7.2.3 FirstCluster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1383">7.2.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1384">Il campo FirstCluster deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry primario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1384">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1385">Questo campo contiene l'indice del primo cluster della catena del cluster, come descritto dal FAT, che ospita la tabella del case.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1385">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Up-case Table.</span></span>

#### <a name="724-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-1386">7.2.4-campo DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1386">7.2.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1387">Il campo datacluster deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry primario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1387">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="725-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-1388">7.2.5-tabella del case</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1388">7.2.5 Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1389">Una tabella del case è una serie di mapping di caratteri Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1389">An up-case table is a series of Unicode character mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1390">Un mapping di caratteri è costituito da un campo a 2 byte, con l'indice del campo nella tabella del case che rappresenta il carattere Unicode per cui deve essere eseguita la combinazione di maiuscole e minuscole e il campo a 2 byte che rappresenta il carattere Unicode in maiuscolo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1390">A character mapping consists of a 2-byte field, with the index of the field in the up-case table representing the Unicode character to be up-cased, and the 2-byte field representing the up-cased Unicode character.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1391">I primi 128 caratteri Unicode hanno mapping obbligatori (vedere la [tabella 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1391">The first 128 Unicode characters have mandatory mappings (see [Table 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1392">Una tabella del case con qualsiasi altro mapping di caratteri per uno dei primi 128 caratteri Unicode non è valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1392">An up-case table which has any other character mapping for any of the first 128 Unicode characters is invalid.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1393">Le implementazioni che supportano solo i caratteri dell'intervallo di mapping obbligatorio potrebbero ignorare i mapping del resto della tabella del case.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1393">Implementations which only support characters from the mandatory mapping range may ignore the mappings of the rest of the up-case table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1394">Tali implementazioni utilizzeranno solo i caratteri dell'intervallo di mapping obbligatorio durante la creazione o la ridenominazione dei file (tramite la voce di directory del nome file, vedere la [sezione 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1394">Such implementations shall only use characters from the mandatory mapping range when creating or renaming files (via the File Name directory entry, see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1395">Quando si esegue il decompressione di nomi di file esistenti, tali implementazioni non devono essere presenti nell'intervallo di mapping non obbligatorio, ma devono essere manomesse nel nome del file in maiuscolo e minuscolo risultante. si tratta di una maiuscola parziale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1395">When up-casing existing file names, such implementations shall not up-case characters from the non-mandatory mapping range, but shall leave them intact in the resulting up-cased file name (this is a partial up-casing).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1396">Quando si confrontano i nomi di file, tali implementazioni tratteranno i nomi di file che differiscono dal nome sotto il confronto solo per i caratteri Unicode dall'intervallo di mapping non obbligatorio come equivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1396">When comparing file names, such implementations shall treat file names which differ from the name under comparison only by Unicode characters from the non-mandatory mapping range as equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1397">Sebbene tali nomi di file siano potenzialmente equivalenti, tali implementazioni non possono garantire che il nome del file con il nome completo non entri in conflitto con il nome sotto il confronto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1397">While such file names are only potentially equivalent, such implementations cannot ensure the fully up-cased file name does not collide with the name under comparison.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1517">**0060h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1517">**0060h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1518">0060h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1518">0060h</span></span>             | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1519">**0041h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1519">**0041h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1520">**0042h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1520">**0042h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1521">**0043h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1521">**0043h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1522">**0044h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1522">**0044h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1523">**0045h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1523">**0045h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1524">**0046h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1524">**0046h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1525">**0047h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1525">**0047h**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1526">**0068h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1526">**0068h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1527">**0048h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1527">**0048h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1528">**0049h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1528">**0049h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1529">**004Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1529">**004Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1530">**004Bh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1530">**004Bh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1531">**004Ch**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1531">**004Ch**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1532">**004Dh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1532">**004Dh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1533">**004Eh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1533">**004Eh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1534">**004Fh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1534">**004Fh**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1535">**0070h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1535">**0070h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1536">**0050h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1536">**0050h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1537">**0051h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1537">**0051h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1538">**0052h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1538">**0052h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1539">**0053h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1539">**0053h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1540">**0054h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1540">**0054h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1541">**0055h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1541">**0055h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1542">**0056h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1542">**0056h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1543">**0057h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1543">**0057h**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1544">**0078h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1544">**0078h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1545">**0058h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1545">**0058h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1546">**0059h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1546">**0059h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1547">**005Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1547">**005Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1548">007Bh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1548">007Bh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1549">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1549">007Ch</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1550">007Dh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1550">007Dh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1551">007Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1551">007Eh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1552">007Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1552">007Fh</span></span>     |

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1553">**Nota: le voci con mapping dei case non di identità sono in grassetto.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1553">**(Note: entries with non-identity up-case mappings are in bold)**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1554">Quando si formatta un volume, le implementazioni possono generare una tabella del case in un formato compresso usando la compressione del mapping delle identità, poiché una parte grande dello spazio dei caratteri Unicode non ha alcun concetto di caso (ovvero i caratteri "minuscole" e "maiuscole" sono equivalenti).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1554">Upon formatting a volume, implementations may generate an up-case table in a compressed format using identity-mapping compression, since a large portion of the Unicode character space has no concept of case (which means the "lower-case" and "upper-case" characters are equivalent).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1555">Le implementazioni comprimeno una tabella del case, rappresentando una serie di mapping di identità con il valore FFFFh seguito dal numero di mapping di identità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1555">Implementations compress an up-case table by representing a series of identity mappings with the value FFFFh followed with the number of identity mappings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1556">Un'implementazione, ad esempio, può rappresentare i primi mapping di caratteri 100 (64H) con le otto voci seguenti di una tabella del case in formato compresso:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1556">For example, an implementation may represent the first 100 (64h) character mappings with the following eight entries of a compressed up-case table:</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1557">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1557">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1558">Le prime due voci indicano che i primi 97 caratteri (61H) (da 0000h a 0060h) hanno mapping di identità.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1558">The first two entries indicate the first 97 (61h) characters (from 0000h to 0060h) have identity mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1559">I caratteri successivi, 0061h tramite 0063h, vengono mappati ai caratteri rispettivamente 0041h tramite 0043h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1559">The subsequent characters, 0061h through 0063h, map to characters 0041h through 0043h, respectively.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1560">La possibilità di fornire una tabella del case in formato compresso alla formattazione di un volume è facoltativa.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1560">The ability to provide a compressed up-case table upon formatting a volume is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1561">Tuttavia, la possibilità di interpretare sia una tabella del case non compressa che una tabella del case compressa è obbligatoria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1561">However, the ability to interpret both an uncompressed and a compressed up-case table is mandatory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-1562">Il valore del campo TableChecksum è sempre conforme al modo in cui esiste la tabella del case nel volume, che può essere in formato compresso o non compresso.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1562">The value of the TableChecksum field always conforms to how the up-case table exists on the volume, which may be in either compressed or uncompressed format.</span></span>

##### <a name="7251-recommended-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-1563">7.2.5.1-tabella del case consigliata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1563">7.2.5.1 Recommended Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1564">Quando si formatta un volume, le implementazioni devono registrare la tabella del caso non consigliata in formato compresso (vedere la [tabella 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), per la quale il valore del campo TableChecksum è E619D30Dh.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1564">When formatting a volume, implementations should record the recommended up-case table in compressed format (see [Table 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), for which the value of the TableChecksum field is E619D30Dh.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-1565">Se un'implementazione definisce la propria tabella del case, compressa o non compressa, la tabella coprirà l'intervallo di caratteri Unicode completo (dai codici carattere 0000h a FFFFh inclusivo).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-1565">If an implementation defines its own up-case table, either compressed or uncompressed, then that table shall cover the complete Unicode character range (from character codes 0000h to FFFFh inclusive).</span></span>

### <a name="73-volume-label-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-4860">Voce di directory dell'etichetta del volume 7,3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4860">7.3 Volume Label Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-4861">L'etichetta del volume è una stringa Unicode che consente agli utenti finali di distinguere i volumi di archiviazione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4861">The Volume Label is a Unicode string which enables end users to distinguish their storage volumes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4862">Nel file system exFAT l'etichetta del volume esiste come voce di directory primaria critica nella directory radice (vedere la [tabella 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4862">In the exFAT file system, the Volume Label exists as a critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4863">Il numero di voci di directory dell'etichetta volume valido è compreso tra 0 e 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4863">The valid number of Volume Label directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

#### <a name="732-charactercount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-4899">Campo 7.3.2 CharacterCount</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4899">7.3.2 CharacterCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-4901">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4901">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4902">Almeno 0, che indica che la stringa Unicode ha una lunghezza pari a 0 caratteri (che equivale a nessuna etichetta del volume)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4902">At least 0, which means the Unicode string is 0 characters long (which is the equivalent of no volume label)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4903">Al massimo 11, che significa che la stringa Unicode ha una lunghezza di 11 caratteri</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4903">At most 11, which means the Unicode string is 11 characters long</span></span>

#### <a name="733-volumelabel-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-4904">Campo 7.3.3 VolumeLabel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4904">7.3.3 VolumeLabel Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-4905">Il campo VolumeLabel deve contenere una stringa Unicode, ovvero il nome descrittivo del volume.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4905">The VolumeLabel field shall contain a Unicode string, which is the user-friendly name of the volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4906">Il campo VolumeLabel contiene lo stesso set di caratteri non validi del campo FileName della voce di directory nome file (vedere la [sezione 7.7.3](#773-filename-field)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4906">The VolumeLabel field has the same set of invalid characters as the FileName field of the File Name directory entry (see [Section 7.7.3](#773-filename-field)).</span></span>

### <a name="74-file-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-4907">7,4 voce directory file</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4907">7.4 File Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-4908">Le voci della directory di file descrivono file e directory.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4908">File directory entries describe files and directories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4909">Si tratta di voci di directory primarie critiche e qualsiasi directory può contenere zero o più voci di directory di file (vedere la [tabella 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4909">They are critical primary directory entries and any directory may contain zero or more File directory entries (see [Table 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-4910">Affinché una voce di directory di file sia valida, una voce di directory di estensione del flusso e almeno una voce di directory di nome file deve seguire immediatamente la voce della directory di file (vedere rispettivamente la [sezione 7,6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) e la [sezione 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4910">For a File directory entry to be valid, exactly one Stream Extension directory entry and at least one File Name directory entry must immediately follow the File directory entry (see [Section 7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) and [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry), respectively).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-4911">**Tabella 27 file DirectoryEntry**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-4911">**Table 27 File DirectoryEntry**</span></span>

<table>

#### <a name="745-createtimestamp-create10msincrement-and-createutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5027">Campi 7.4.5 CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement e CreateUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5027">7.4.5 CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement, and CreateUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5028">In combinazione, i campi CreateTimestamp e CreateTime10msIncrement descrivono la data e l'ora locali in cui è stata creata la directory o il file specificato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5028">In combination, the CreateTimestamp and CreateTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the given file/directory was created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5029">Il campo CreateUtcOffset descrive l'offset della data e dell'ora locali dall'ora UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5029">The CreateUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5030">Le implementazioni devono impostare questi campi al momento della creazione del set di voci di directory specificato.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5030">Implementations shall set these fields upon creation of the given directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5031">Questi campi devono essere conformi alle definizioni dei campi timestamp, 10msIncrement e UtcOffset (vedere rispettivamente la sezione [7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), la [sezione 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)e la [sezione 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5031">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="746-lastmodifiedtimestamp-lastmodified10msincrement-and-lastmodifiedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5032">Campi 7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement e LastModifiedUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5032">7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement, and LastModifiedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5033">In combinazione, i campi LastModifiedTimestamp e LastModifiedTime10msIncrement descrivono la data e l'ora locali in cui è stato modificato l'ultima modifica del contenuto di tutti i cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5033">In combination, the LastModifiedTimestamp and LastModifiedTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5034">Il campo LastModifiedUtcOffset descrive l'offset della data e dell'ora locali dall'ora UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5034">The LastModifiedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5035">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare i campi seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5035">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5036">Dopo aver modificato il contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata (ad eccezione dei contenuti presenti oltre il punto in cui viene descritto il campo ValidDataLength)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5036">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the point the ValidDataLength field describes)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5037">Quando si modificano i valori dei campi ValidDataLength o DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5037">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5038">Questi campi devono essere conformi alle definizioni dei campi timestamp, 10msIncrement e UtcOffset (vedere rispettivamente la sezione [7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), la [sezione 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)e la [sezione 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5038">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="747-lastaccessedtimestamp-and-lastaccessedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5039">Campi 7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp e LastAccessedUtcOffset</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5039">7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp and LastAccessedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5040">Il campo LastAccessedTimestamp descrivono la data e l'ora locali in cui è stato eseguito l'ultimo accesso al contenuto di uno dei cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5040">The LastAccessedTimestamp field shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5041">Il campo LastAccessedUtcOffset descrive l'offset della data e dell'ora locali dall'ora UTC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5041">The LastAccessedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5042">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare i campi seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5042">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5043">Dopo aver modificato il contenuto di tutti i cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata (ad eccezione dei contenuti presenti oltre il ValidDataLength)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5043">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the ValidDataLength)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5044">Quando si modificano i valori dei campi ValidDataLength o DataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5044">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5045">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare questi campi dopo la lettura del contenuto di tutti i cluster associati alla voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5045">Implementations should update these fields after reading the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5046">Questi campi devono essere conformi alle definizioni dei campi timestamp e UtcOffset (vedere rispettivamente la [sezione 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) e la [sezione 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5046">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5048">I campi timestamp descrivono la data e l'ora locali, fino a una risoluzione di due secondi (vedere la [tabella 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5048">Timestamp fields describe both local date and time, down to a two-second resolution (see [Table 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7481-doubleseconds-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5080">Campo 7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5080">7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5081">Il campo DoubleSeconds descrive la parte relativa ai secondi del campo timestamp, in multipli di due secondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5081">The DoubleSeconds field shall describe the seconds portion of the Timestamp field, in two-second multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5082">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5082">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5083">0, che rappresenta 0 secondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5083">0, which represents 0 seconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5084">29, che rappresenta 58 secondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5084">29, which represents 58 seconds</span></span>

##### <a name="7482-minute-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5085">Campo 7.4.8.2 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5085">7.4.8.2 Minute Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5086">Il campo minuti descrivono la parte relativa ai minuti del campo timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5086">The Minute field shall describe the minutes portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5087">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5087">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5088">0, che rappresenta 0 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5088">0, which represents 0 minutes</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5089">59, che rappresenta 59 minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5089">59, which represents 59 minutes</span></span>

##### <a name="7483-hour-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5090">Campo 7.4.8.3 hour</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5090">7.4.8.3 Hour Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5091">Il campo hour descriva la parte hours del campo timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5091">The Hour field shall describe the hours portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5092">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5092">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5093">0, che rappresenta 00:00 ore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5093">0, which represents 00:00 hours</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5094">23, che rappresenta 23:00 ore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5094">23, which represents 23:00 hours</span></span>

##### <a name="7484-day-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5095">Campo 7.4.8.4 Day</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5095">7.4.8.4 Day Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5096">Il campo Day descrivono la parte relativa al giorno del campo timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5096">The Day field shall describe the day portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5097">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5097">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5098">1, ovvero il primo giorno del mese specificato</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5098">1, which is the first day of the given month</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5099">Ultimo giorno del mese specificato (il mese specificato definisce il numero di giorni validi)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5099">The last day of the given month (the given month defines the number of valid days)</span></span>

##### <a name="7485-month-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5100">Campo 7.4.8.5 month</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5100">7.4.8.5 Month Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5101">Il campo month descriva la porzione month del campo timestamp.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5101">The Month field shall describe the month portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5102">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5102">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5103">Almeno 1, che rappresenta il gennaio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5103">At least 1, which represents January</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5104">Al massimo 12, che rappresenta dicembre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5104">At most 12, which represents December</span></span>

##### <a name="7486-year-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5105">Campo 7.4.8.6 year</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5105">7.4.8.6 Year Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5106">Il campo Year descriva la parte relativa all'anno del campo timestamp rispetto all'anno 1980.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5106">The Year field shall describe the year portion of the Timestamp field, relative to the year 1980.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5107">Questo campo rappresenta l'anno 1980 con il valore 0 e l'anno 2107 con il valore 127.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5107">This field represents the year 1980 with the value 0 and the year 2107 with the value 127.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5108">Tutti i valori possibili per questo campo sono validi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5108">All possible values for this field are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="749-10msincrement-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5109">Campi 10msIncrement di 7.4.9</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5109">7.4.9 10msIncrement Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5110">i campi 10msIncrement forniscono ulteriore risoluzione del tempo ai campi timestamp corrispondenti nei multipli di dieci millisecondi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5110">10msIncrement fields shall provide additional time resolution to their corresponding Timestamp fields in ten-millisecond multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5111">L'intervallo valido di valori per questi campi deve essere:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5111">The valid range of values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5112">Almeno 0, che rappresenta 0 millisecondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5112">At least 0, which represents 0 milliseconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5113">Al massimo 199, che rappresenta 1990 millisecondi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5113">At most 199, which represents 1990 milliseconds</span></span>

#### <a name="7410-utcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5114">Campi UtcOffset di 7.4.10</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5114">7.4.10 UtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5115">I campi UtcOffset (vedere la [tabella 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) descrivono l'offset dall'ora UTC alla data e all'ora locali in cui vengono descritti i campi timestamp e 10msIncrement corrispondenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5115">UtcOffset fields (see [Table 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) shall describe the offset from UTC to the local date and time their corresponding Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields describe.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5116">L'offset dall'ora UTC alla data e all'ora locali include gli effetti dei fusi orari e altre rettifiche di data e ora, ad esempio le modifiche all'ora legale e all'ora dell'ora legale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5116">The offset from UTC to the local date and time includes the effects of time zones and other date-time adjustments, such as daylight saving and regional summer time changes.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5180">La data e l'ora locali sono in realtà identiche all'ora UTC, nel qual caso il valore del campo OffsetValid sarà 1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5180">Local date and time are actually the same as UTC, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5181">La data e l'ora locali non sono note, nel qual caso il valore del campo OffsetValid sarà 1 e le implementazioni considereranno UTC come data e ora locali</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5181">Local date and time are not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1 and implementations shall consider UTC to be local date and time</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5182">L'ora UTC non è nota, nel qual caso il valore del campo OffsetValid sarà 0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5182">UTC is not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 0</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5183">Se l'offset di data e ora locale rispetto all'ora UTC non è un multiplo di intervalli di 15 minuti, le implementazioni registreranno 00h nel campo OffsetFromUtc e considereranno UTC come data e ora locali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5183">If the local date and time offset from UTC happens to not be a multiple of 15 minute intervals, then implementations shall record 00h in the OffsetFromUtc field and shall consider UTC to be local date and time.</span></span>

##### <a name="74102-offsetvalid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5184">Campo 7.4.10.2 OffsetValid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5184">7.4.10.2 OffsetValid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5185">Il campo OffsetValid indica se il contenuto del campo OffsetFromUtc è valido o meno, come indicato di seguito:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5185">The OffsetValid field shall describe whether the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid or not, as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5186">0, che indica che il contenuto del campo OffsetFromUtc non è valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5186">0, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are invalid</span></span>
    > <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5187">e sarà 00h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5187">and shall be 00h</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5188">1, che indica che il contenuto del campo OffsetFromUtc è valido</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5188">1, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5189">Le implementazioni devono impostare questo campo solo sul valore 0 quando l'ora UTC non è disponibile per il calcolo del valore del campo OffsetFromUtc.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5189">Implementations should only set this field to the value 0 when UTC is not available for computing the value of the OffsetFromUtc field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5190">Se questo campo contiene il valore 0, le implementazioni devono considerare i campi timestamp e 10msIncrement come aventi lo stesso offset UTC della data e dell'ora locali correnti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5190">If this field contains the value 0, then implementations shall treat the Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields as having the same UTC offset as the current local date and time.</span></span>

### <a name="75-volume-guid-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5191">7,5 voce directory GUID volume</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5191">7.5 Volume GUID Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5192">La voce della directory GUID del volume contiene un GUID che consente alle implementazioni di distinguere i volumi in modo univoco e a livello di codice.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5192">The Volume GUID directory entry contains a GUID which enables implementations to uniquely and programmatically distinguish volumes.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5193">Il GUID del volume esiste come voce di directory primaria benigna nella directory radice (vedere la [tabella 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5193">The Volume GUID exists as a benign primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5194">Il numero di voci della directory GUID del volume valido è compreso tra 0 e 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5194">The valid number of Volume GUID directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

### <a name="76-stream-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5253">Voce di directory dell'estensione di flusso 7,6</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5253">7.6 Stream Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5256">Inoltre, questa voce di directory è valida solo se segue immediatamente la voce della directory di file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5256">Further, this directory entry is valid only if it immediately follows the File directory entry.</span></span>

#### <a name="763-namelength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5323">Campo 7.6.3 NameLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5323">7.6.3 NameLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5324">Il campo NameLength conterrà la lunghezza della stringa Unicode in cui sono contenute le voci di directory del nome file successive (vedere la [sezione 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) collettivamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5324">The NameLength field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the subsequent File Name directory entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) collectively contain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5325">L'intervallo valido di valori per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5325">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5326">Almeno 1, ovvero il nome file più breve possibile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5326">At least 1, which is the shortest possible file name</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5327">Al massimo 255, che è il nome file più lungo possibile</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5327">At most 255, which is the longest possible file name</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5328">Il valore del campo NameLength influiscono anche sulle voci di directory del nome del file numerico (vedere la [sezione 7,7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5328">The value of the NameLength field also affects the number File Name Directory Entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span>

#### <a name="764-namehash-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5329">Campo 7.6.4 NameHash</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5329">7.6.4 NameHash Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5330">Il campo NameHash conterrà un hash a 2 byte (vedere la [Figura 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation)) del nome del file con maiuscole/minuscole.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5330">The NameHash field shall contain a 2-byte hash (see [Figure 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation)) of the up-cased file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5331">Questo consente alle implementazioni di eseguire un confronto rapido quando si cerca un file in base al nome.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5331">This enables implementations to perform a quick comparison when searching for a file by name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5332">Un aspetto importante è che il NameHash fornisce una verifica della mancata corrispondenza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5332">Importantly, the NameHash provides a sure verification of a mismatch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5333">Le implementazioni devono verificare che tutte le corrispondenze di NameHash con un confronto tra il nome del file in questione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5333">Implementations shall verify all NameHash matches with a comparison of the up-cased file name.</span></span>

<div id="figure-4-namehash-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5334">**Figura 4 calcolo NameHash**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5334">**Figure 4 NameHash Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt16 NameHash
(
    WCHAR * FileName,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-cased file name
    UCHAR   NameLength
)
{
    UCHAR  * Buffer = (UCHAR *)FileName;
    UInt16   NumberOfBytes = (UInt16)NameLength * 2;
    UInt16   Hash = 0;
    UInt16   Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        Hash = ((Hash&1) ? 0x8000 : 0) + (Hash>>1) + (UInt16)Buffer[Index];
    }
    return Hash;
}
```

#### <a name="765-validdatalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5335">Campo 7.6.5 ValidDataLength</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5335">7.6.5 ValidDataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5336">Il campo ValidDataLength descrive la distanza di scrittura dei dati utente del flusso di dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5336">The ValidDataLength field shall describe how far into the data stream user data has been written.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5337">Le implementazioni devono aggiornare questo campo Man mano che scrivono i dati nel flusso di dati.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5337">Implementations shall update this field as they write data further out into the data stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5338">Sul supporto di archiviazione i dati tra la lunghezza dei dati valida e la lunghezza dei dati del flusso di dati non sono definiti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5338">On the storage media, the data between the valid data length and the data length of the data stream is undefined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5339">Le implementazioni devono restituire zeri per le operazioni di lettura oltre la lunghezza dei dati valida.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5339">Implementations shall return zeroes for read operations beyond the valid data length.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5340">Se la voce della directory di file corrispondente descrive una directory, l'unico valore valido per questo campo è uguale al valore del campo DATALENGTH.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5340">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the only valid value for this field is equal to the value of the DataLength field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5341">In caso contrario, l'intervallo di valori validi per questo campo sarà:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5341">Otherwise, the range of valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5342">Almeno 0, che indica che nessun dato utente è stato scritto nel flusso di dati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5342">At least 0, which means no user data has been written out to the data stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5343">Al massimo DATALENGTH, che indica che i dati utente sono stati scritti nell'intera lunghezza del flusso di dati</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5343">At most DataLength, which means user data has been written out to the entire length of the data stream</span></span>

### <a name="77-file-name-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5351">7,7 voce directory nome file</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5351">7.7 File Name Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5352">Le voci di directory del nome file sono voci di directory secondarie critiche nei set di voci di directory di file (vedere la [tabella 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5352">File Name directory entries are critical secondary directory entries in File directory entry sets (see [Table 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5353">Il numero valido di voci della directory dei nomi di file in un set di voci della directory di file è NameLength/15, arrotondato per eccesso al numero intero più vicino.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5353">The valid number of File Name directory entries in a File directory entry set is NameLength / 15, rounded up to the nearest integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5354">Inoltre, le voci di directory dei nomi di file sono valide solo se seguono immediatamente la voce della directory dell'estensione di flusso come serie consecutiva.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5354">Further, File Name directory entries are valid only if they immediately follow the Stream Extension directory entry as a consecutive series.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5355">Le voci di directory del nome file si combinano per formare il nome file per il set di voci della directory di file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5355">File Name directory entries combine to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5356">Tutti gli elementi figlio di una determinata voce di directory avranno set di voci di directory di nomi file univoci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5356">All children of a given directory entry shall have unique File Name Directory Entry Sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5357">In altre parole, è possibile che non esistano nomi di file o directory duplicati dopo l'uso di maiuscole e minuscole in una directory.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5357">That is to say there can be no duplicate file or directory names after up-casing within any one directory.</span></span>

##### <a name="7712-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5382">Campo 7.7.1.2 TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5382">7.7.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5384">Per la voce della directory dell'estensione del flusso, il valore valido per questo campo è 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5384">For the Stream Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7713-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5385">Campo 7.7.1.3 TypeCategory</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5385">7.7.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5386">Il campo TypeCategory deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1.3](#6413-typecategory-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5386">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.3](#6413-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7714-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5387">Campo 7.7.1.4 InUse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5387">7.7.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5388">Il campo InUse deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1.4](#6414-inuse-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5388">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.4](#6414-inuse-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="772-generalsecondaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5389">Campo 7.7.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5389">7.7.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5390">Il campo GeneralSecondaryFlags deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere la [sezione 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) e definisce il contenuto del campo CustomDefined da riservare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5390">The GeneralSecondaryFlags field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) and defines the contents of the CustomDefined field to be reserved.</span></span>

##### <a name="7721-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5391">Campo 7.7.2.1 AllocationPossible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5391">7.7.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5392">Il campo AllocationPossible deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5392">The AllocationPossible field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5393">Per la voce della directory dell'estensione del flusso, il valore valido per questo campo è 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5393">For the Stream Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7722-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5394">Campo 7.7.2.2 NoFatChain</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5394">7.7.2.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5395">Il campo NoFatChain deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5395">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="773-filename-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5396">Campo 7.7.3 FileName</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5396">7.7.3 FileName Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5397">Il campo FileName deve contenere una stringa Unicode, che è una parte del nome file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5397">The FileName field shall contain a Unicode string, which is a portion of the file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5398">Nelle voci di directory del nome del file dell'ordine esistono in un set di voci di directory di file, i campi FileName vengono concatenati per formare il nome file per il set di voci della directory di file.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5398">In the order File Name directory entries exist in a File directory entry set, FileName fields concatenate to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5399">Data la lunghezza del campo FileName, 15 caratteri e il numero massimo di voci di directory dei nomi file, 17, la lunghezza massima del nome file concatenato finale è</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5399">Given the length of the FileName field, 15 characters, and the maximum number of File Name directory entries, 17, the maximum length of the final, concatenated file name is</span></span>
255.

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5400">Il nome del file concatenato ha lo stesso set di caratteri non validi di altri file System basati su FAT (vedere la [tabella 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5400">The concatenated file name has the same set of illegal characters as other FAT-based file systems (see [Table 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5401">Le implementazioni devono impostare i caratteri inutilizzati dei campi FileName sul valore 0000h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5401">Implementations should set the unused characters of FileName fields to the value 0000h.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5491">I nomi file "." e ".." hanno il significato speciale "questa directory" e "directory contenitore", rispettivamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5491">The file names "." and ".." have the special meaning of "this directory" and "containing directory", respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5492">Le implementazioni non devono registrare uno di questi nomi di file riservati nel campo FileName.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5492">Implementations shall not record either of these reserved file names in the FileName field.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5493">Tuttavia, le implementazioni possono generare questi due nomi file nelle visualizzazioni directory per fare riferimento alla directory elencata e alla directory che lo contiene.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5493">However, implementations may generate these two file names in directory listings to refer to the directory being listed and the containing directory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5494">Le implementazioni possono voler limitare i nomi di file e directory solo al set di caratteri ASCII.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5494">Implementations may wish to restrict file and directory names to just the ASCII character set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5495">In tal caso, è necessario limitare l'utilizzo di caratteri all'intervallo di caratteri validi nelle prime 128 voci Unicode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5495">If so they should limit their character use to the range of valid characters in the first 128 Unicode entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5496">Devono comunque archiviare i nomi di file e directory in Unicode nel volume e tradurli in/da ASCII/Unicode in caso di interazione con l'utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5496">They must still store file and directory names in Unicode on the volume and translate to/from ASCII/Unicode when interfacing with the user.</span></span>

### <a name="78-vendor-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5497">Voce di directory dell'estensione del fornitore 7,8</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5497">7.8 Vendor Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5498">La voce della directory di estensione del fornitore è una voce di directory secondaria benigna nei set di voci di directory di file (vedere la [tabella 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5498">The Vendor Extension directory entry is a benign secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5499">Un set di voci di directory di file può contenere un numero qualsiasi di voci di directory di estensione del fornitore, fino al limite di voci di directory secondarie, meno il numero di altre voci della directory secondaria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5499">A File directory entry set may contain any number of Vendor Extension directory entries, up to the limit of secondary directory entries, less the number of other secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5500">Inoltre, le voci di directory di estensione del fornitore sono valide solo se non precedono le voci della directory di estensione del flusso e dei nomi file richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5500">Further, Vendor Extension directory entries are valid only if they do not precede the required Stream Extension and File Name directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5501">Le voci di directory di estensione del fornitore consentono ai fornitori di avere voci di directory specifiche del fornitore univoche nei singoli set di voci di directory di file tramite il campo VendorGuid (vedere la [tabella 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5501">Vendor Extension directory entries enable vendors to have unique, vendor-specific directory entries in individual File directory entry sets via the VendorGuid field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5502">Le voci di directory univoche consentono ai fornitori di estendere il file system di exFAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5502">Unique directory entries effectively enable vendors to extend the exFAT file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5503">I fornitori possono definire il contenuto del campo VendorDefined (vedere la [tabella 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5503">Vendors may define the contents of the VendorDefined field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5504">Le implementazioni dei fornitori possono mantenere il contenuto del campo VendorDefined e possono fornire funzionalità specifiche del fornitore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5504">Vendor implementations may maintain the contents of the VendorDefined field and may provide vendor-specific functionality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5505">Le implementazioni che non riconoscono il GUID di una voce di directory dell'estensione del fornitore considereranno la voce della directory uguale a qualsiasi altra voce di directory secondaria benigna non riconosciuta (vedere la [sezione 8,2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5505">Implementations which do not recognize the GUID of a Vendor Extension directory entry shall treat the directory entry the same as any other unrecognized benign secondary directory entry (see [Section 8.2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span></span>

#### <a name="781-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5529">Campo 7.8.1 EntryType</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5529">7.8.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5530">Il campo EntryType deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1](#641-entrytype-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5530">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1](#641-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7811-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5531">Campo TypeCode 7.8.1.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5531">7.8.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5532">Il campo TypeCode deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1.1](#6411-typecode-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5532">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.1](#6411-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5533">Per la voce della directory dell'estensione del fornitore, il valore valido per questo campo è 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5533">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7812-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5534">Campo 7.8.1.2 TypeImportance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5534">7.8.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5535">Il campo TypeImportance deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1.2](#6412-typeimportance-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5535">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.2](#6412-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5536">Per la voce della directory dell'estensione del fornitore, il valore valido per questo campo è 1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5536">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="7813-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5537">Campo 7.8.1.3 TypeCategory</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5537">7.8.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5538">Il campo TypeCategory deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1.3](#6413-typecategory-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5538">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.3](#6413-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7814-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5539">Campo 7.8.1.4 InUse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5539">7.8.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5540">Il campo InUse deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.1.4](#6414-inuse-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5540">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.4](#6414-inuse-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="782-generalsecondaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5541">Campo 7.8.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5541">7.8.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5542">Il campo GeneralSecondaryFlags deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico (vedere la [sezione 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) e definisce il contenuto del campo CustomDefined da riservare.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5542">The GeneralSecondaryFlags field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) and defines the contents of the CustomDefined field to be reserved.</span></span>

##### <a name="7821-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5543">Campo 7.8.2.1 AllocationPossible</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5543">7.8.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5544">Il campo AllocationPossible deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5544">The AllocationPossible field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5545">Per la voce della directory dell'estensione del fornitore, il valore valido per questo campo è 0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5545">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7822-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5546">Campo 7.8.2.2 NoFatChain</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5546">7.8.2.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5547">Il campo NoFatChain deve essere conforme alla definizione fornita nel modello DirectoryEntry secondario generico. vedere la [sezione 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5547">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="783-vendorguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5548">Campo 7.8.3 VendorGuid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5548">7.8.3 VendorGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5549">Il campo VendorGuid deve contenere un GUID che identifica in modo univoco l'estensione del fornitore specificata.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5549">The VendorGuid field shall contain a GUID which uniquely identifies the given Vendor Extension.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5550">Tutti i valori possibili per questo campo sono validi, ad eccezione del GUID null, ovvero {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000} .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5550">All possible values for this field are valid, except the null GUID, which is {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000}.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5551">Tuttavia, i fornitori devono usare uno strumento di generazione GUID, ad esempio GuidGen.exe, per selezionare un GUID durante la definizione delle estensioni.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5551">However, vendors should use a GUID-generating tool, such as GuidGen.exe, to select a GUID when defining their extensions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5552">Il valore di questo campo determina la struttura specifica del fornitore del campo VendorDefined.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5552">The value of this field determines the vendor-specific structure of the VendorDefined field.</span></span>

### <a name="79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5553">7,9 voce di directory di allocazione fornitore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5553">7.9 Vendor Allocation Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5554">La voce della directory di allocazione del fornitore è una voce di directory secondaria benigna nei set di voci di directory di file (vedere la [tabella 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5554">The Vendor Allocation directory entry is a benign secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5555">Un set di voci della directory di file può contenere un numero qualsiasi di voci di directory di allocazione del fornitore, fino al limite di voci della directory secondaria, minore il numero di altre voci della directory secondaria.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5555">A File directory entry set may contain any number of Vendor Allocation directory entries, up to the limit of secondary directory entries, less the number of other secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5556">Inoltre, le voci di directory di allocazione del fornitore sono valide solo se non precedono le voci della directory di estensione del flusso e dei nomi file richieste.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5556">Further, Vendor Allocation directory entries are valid only if they do not precede the required Stream Extension and File Name directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5557">Le voci di directory di allocazione del fornitore consentono ai fornitori di avere voci di directory specifiche del fornitore univoche nei singoli set di voci di directory di file tramite il campo VendorGuid (vedere la [tabella 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5557">Vendor Allocation directory entries enable vendors to have unique, vendor-specific directory entries in individual File directory entry sets via the VendorGuid field (see [Table 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5558">Le voci di directory univoche consentono ai fornitori di estendere il file system di exFAT.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5558">Unique directory entries effectively enable vendors to extend the exFAT file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5559">I fornitori possono definire il contenuto dei cluster associati, se presenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5559">Vendors may define the contents of the associated clusters, if any exist.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4039c-5560">Le implementazioni del fornitore possono mantenere il contenuto dei cluster associati, se presente, e possono fornire funzionalità specifiche del fornitore.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5560">Vendor implementations may maintain the contents of the associated clusters, if any, and may provide vendor-specific functionality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5561">Le implementazioni che non riconoscono il GUID di una voce di directory di allocazione del fornitore devono considerare la voce di directory come qualsiasi altra voce di directory secondaria benigna non riconosciuta (vedere la [sezione 8,2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5561">Implementations which do not recognize the GUID of a Vendor Allocation directory entry shall treat the directory entry the same as any other unrecognized benign secondary directory entry (see [Section 8.2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span></span>

#### <a name="793-vendorguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="4039c-5612">Campo 7.9.3 VendorGuid</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5612">7.9.3 VendorGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4039c-5616">Il valore di questo campo determina la struttura specifica del fornitore del contenuto dei cluster associati, se presenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4039c-5616">The value of this field determines the vendor-specific structure of the contents of the associated clusters, if any exist.</span></span>
